beginSubroutine: s32'ServantPickUp'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg2)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(-80000)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(180000)
          calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_Y), (SELF), (PLAYER), (STACK1), (PLAYER)

beginSubroutine: s32'ReleaseGhostCancel'
  if: Mem(IsNamaDashiSkill)
    enableBurst: 1
    forceEnableBlueRomanCancel: 1
  endIf: 
  enableWhiffCancel: 1
  addWhiffCancelOption: s32'ElysionDriver'
  addWhiffCancelOption: s32'PowerUp_S'
  addWhiffCancelOption: s32'PowerUp_HS'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'ReleaseGhostCancelEnd'
  if: Mem(IsNamaDashiSkill)
    enableBurst: 0
    forceEnableBlueRomanCancel: 0
  endIf: 
  removeWhiffCancelOption: s32'ElysionDriver'
  removeWhiffCancelOption: s32'PowerUp_S'
  removeWhiffCancelOption: s32'PowerUp_HS'
endSubroutine:

      sendSignalName: 4, s32'Neutral', 0
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(2)
      sendSignalName: 5, s32'Neutral', 0
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(3)
      sendSignalName: 6, s32'Neutral', 0
    endIf: 
    upon: (IDLING)
      exPointFReset: (PLAYER), 0, 410000
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'jko427_00', 2
  callSubroutine: s32'ReleaseGhostCancel'
  sprite: s32'jko427_00', 3
  callSubroutine: s32'ReleaseGhostCancelEnd'
  callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmnAddTensionGG', Val(8), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
  sprite: s32'jko427_01', 3
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
    sendSignalName: 4, s32'Release', 0
    storeValueFromObject: (STACK0), Mem(ObjReg3), (SELF), Val(0)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(2)
    sendSignalName: 5, s32'Release', 0
    storeValueFromObject: (STACK1), Mem(ObjReg3), (SELF), Val(0)
  endIf:
